<td class="text"> In our Current Report on Form 8-K filed with the SEC on December 13, 2022, we reported that we appointed Anindita (Ann) Mukherjee to the Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. Board of Directors, effective January 1, 2023. We are filing this Amendment No. 1 to that Form 8-K to report that our Board of Directors appointed Ms. Mukherjee to serve as a member of the Governance, Membership and Sustainability Committee and a member of the People and Compensation Committee, effective February 2, 2023. Our Board of Directors has made an affirmative determination that Ms.&#160;Mukherjee is independent for purposes of the Nasdaq Stock Market Listing Rules. As previously disclosed in our Form 8-K, there are no transactions between Ms.&#160;Mukherjee and us that would be reportable under Item 404(a) of Regulation&#160;S-K.&#160;Ms.&#160;Mukherjee was not selected pursuant to any arrangement or understanding between her and any other person.<span></span>
</td>

Board of Directors, effective January 1, 2023. We are filing this Amendment No. 1 to that Form 8-K to report that our Board of Directors appointed Ms. Mukherjee to serve as a member of the Governance, Membership and Sustainability Committee and a member of the People and Compensation Committee, effective February 2, 2023. Our Board of Directors has made an affirmative determination that Ms.&#160;Mukherjee is independent for purposes of the Nasdaq Stock Market Listing Rules. As previously disclosed in our Form 8-K, there are no transactions between Ms.&#160;Mukherjee and us that would be reportable under Item 404(a) of Regulation&#160;S-K.&#160;Ms.&#160;Mukherjee was not selected pursuant to any arrangement or understanding between her and any other person.</dei:AmendmentDescription>
